       <tr>
        <td style="border-bottom:1px solid #aaa; padding-bottom:0.5em;">
         Eclipses seen from
         <br/>
         <div class="hlist">
          <ul>
           <li>
            <a class="mw-selflink selflink">
             Australia
            </a>
           </li>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_China" title="List of solar eclipses visible from China">
             China
            </a>
           </li>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_the_Philippines" title="List of solar eclipses visible from the Philippines">
             Philippines
            </a>
           </li>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_Russia" title="List of solar eclipses visible from Russia">
             Russia
            </a>
           </li>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_Ukraine" title="List of solar eclipses visible from Ukraine">
             Ukraine
            </a>
           </li>
           <li>
            <span class="nowrap">
             <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_the_United_Kingdom" title="List of solar eclipses visible from the United Kingdom">
              United Kingdom
             </a>
            </span>
           </li>
           <li>
            <span class="nowrap">
             <a href="/wiki/List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_the_United_States" title="List of solar eclipses visible from the United States">
              United States
             </a>
            </span>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td style="font-size:80%;">
         See also
         <a href="/wiki/Lists_of_lunar_eclipses" title="Lists of lunar eclipses">
          Lists of lunar eclipses
         </a>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <p>
       <b>
        Solar eclipses visible from Australia
       </b>
       are relatively common. A
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipse
       </a>
       occurs when the
       <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">
        Moon
       </a>
       passes between
       <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">
        Earth
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Sun" title="Sun">
        Sun
       </a>
       , thereby totally or partially obscuring Earth's view of the Sun. The shadows of solar eclipses often cross the Australian continent due to its large area of over 7.6 million square kilometers. However a view of
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology_for_central_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        totality
       </a>
       from the continent is rare, with totality occurring over the Australian continent only five times during the
       <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">
        20th century
       </a>
       AD, although it is predicted to occur more frequently, eleven times, during the
       <a href="/wiki/21st_century" title="21st century">
        21st century
       </a>
       AD.
      </p>
      <p>
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Total_and_annular_eclipses">
        Total and annular eclipses
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Total_eclipses">
        Total eclipses
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_Australia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Total eclipses">

        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Total solar eclipses visible on the Australian continent, 1800–2100.

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Annular_eclipses">
        Annular eclipses
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_Australia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Annular eclipses">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Annular solar eclipses visible on the Australian continent, 1800–2100.

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Partial_eclipses">
        Partial eclipses
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_solar_eclipses_visible_from_Australia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Partial eclipses">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Solar eclipses visible partially on the Australian continent.
